padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2352718" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="UGAMark"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2316554"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="UGAMark" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2352718ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2352718" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.87); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2316554">UGAMark</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-11-18"></span><fromunixtime unixtime="1731924830" class="vote-button-legend"></fromunixtime></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is a scent I so wanted to love but, frustratingly, it isn't for me.  Went to Bloomingdales and received card samples from the Parfums de Marly booth, as well as sprays on my wrist of both Greenley and Herod.  On the card, Greenley smells fantastic, if you're into brighter woody scents.  The cedar comes out a lot, almost pine-sappy smelling, in a good way.  But on my skin, it smelled *completely* different.  It smelled exactly like my wife's bottle of PDM Valaya -- a truly amazing scent that I love, but not the notes I wanted after smelling Greenley on the card.  I have never ever had a cologne on a card smell nothing like it on my skin.  Differences, yes, but the DNA is always consistent.  Not with Greenley.  Something about my pheromones or skin must clash with Greenley.  So word to the wise, as with all perfumes/colognes but especially with Greenley, apparently, try it on you and don't rely just on a card spray or anyone else's experiences/descriptons when deciding if this is for you.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Easy to wear and mass appealing</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62101"comment_id="2350312"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Greenley-62101.html?ccid=2350312#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2345830" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2345830" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Chris Simpkins"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1287048"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1287048.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Chris Simpkins" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2345830ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2345830" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.79); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1287048">Chris Simpkins</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-11-11">11/11/24 18:19</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Ugh!  Greenley is an absolute banger!  Yes, initially it smells like an apple shampoo, but give it 30 minutes and it dries down a bit more masculine and woody and the green apple goes more into the background and compliments the musk, cedar and petitgrain perfectly. <br />
<br />
If you think Terre d’Hermes is a “dirty orange,” but like the concept, you will LOVE Greenley.  Terre d’Hermes is a bit more daring and people seem to love or hate it, but there’s just nothing to hate about Greenley. <br />
<br />
In the same vain as Sedley, but the dry down and mids of Greenley are more fresh, apple/woody where the dry down and mids of Sedley seem a bit more, fresh laundry, white T-shirt.  <br />
<br />
This reminds me of Creed Original Vetiver but exchange the ginger in OV with apple and oakmoss. <br />
<br />
Great for spring and summer but I think you can still pull this off in moderate temperatures of fall when everyone is going nuts over caramel apple drinks at their favorite coffee shop.   <br />
<br />
This lasts for 6+ hours on me.  If I was going to dinner after work, I might freshen it up with a couple shots, but otherwise, it lasts pretty well. <br />
<br />
For coastal or beach weather/wear, I might want to go with something more acquatic and marine, but otherwise, this is perfection in a bottle. <br />
<br />
A solid 9/10 for spring, summer and early fall.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62101"comment_id="2345830"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Greenley-62101.html?ccid=2345830#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2345371" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2345164" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="sidalwayssmellsgood"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2001234"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2001234.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="sidalwayssmellsgood" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2345164ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2345164" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2001234">sidalwayssmellsgood</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-11-11">11/11/24 06:15</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Oh, how has no one called this fragrance gourmand!<br />
<br />
Juicy, green, lush: imagine finding a massive green apple, cutting it up, sprinkling some lemon juice on it, taking it out to your balcony to enjoy the cool spring breeze, and just biting into every piece of that green apple while the juices fall on your ultra expensive cardigan.<br />
<br />
This is a sleeper. I feel people don’t do it much justice. Sure, it’s on the same shop rack as Sedley, gets completely ignored because of a Layton, is not on the list of someone shopping for Oajan, and doesn’t come in a shiny bottle like Godolphin. Sure, Creed’s GIT is a more grown-up green fragrance. And sure this doesn’t last too long. But what would I not give to overspray myself over and over again!<br />
<br />
The quality of the ingredients is absolutely magical. Don’t kid yourself. Get this. It’s the only green you need.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62101"comment_id="2345164"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Greenley-62101.html?ccid=2345164#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.78); padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2321004" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="RazerGreg"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1473791"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="RazerGreg" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Oajan-21548.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.21548.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Oajan"title="Oajan"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2321004ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2321004" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.71); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1473791">RazerGreg</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-19">10/19/24 13:27</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I recently tried Greenley by Parfums de Marly, and it reminded me of a cheap aftershave you might find at a discount store. The scent includes bergamot, green apple, mandarin, and cedarwood—ingredients commonly found in many aftershaves. These notes contribute to a fresh, citrusy, and woody profile that feels generic and overly familiar.<br />
<br />
Additionally, Greenley has a synthetic quality, especially in the apple note, which detracts from its uniqueness. I also found that the distinctive profile and DNA of Parfums de Marly are completely missing in this fragrance. While the intention to create a fresh scent is clear, in my opinion, this attempt was a complete fail.<br />
<br />
I strongly recommend trying Greenley before you buy it, as it is not a safe blind buy. If you're looking for a unique and distinctive fragrance, I would recommend Layton instead. Although Layton is a completely different fragrance, it embodies the unique qualities that Parfums de Marly is known for. Unfortunately, I cannot recommend Greenley.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62101"comment_id="2321004"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Greenley-62101.html?ccid=2321004#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2318793" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2318793" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Coletron"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1890245"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1890245.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Coletron" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2318793ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2318793" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1890245">Coletron</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-17">10/17/24 10:25</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Honestly, it's a very disappointing fragrance. The opening is nice at first, very sweet and citrusy. But after a while the smell gets very intrusive. Very good projection and longevity, but the smell alone is not good. Not exaggerating at all, but after having this scent on for a few hours I started to feel nauseous and I was nauseous for the rest of the day. Not a really complex smell, just a very synthetic, sweet citrus fragrance, I don't really even smell the green apple, just piercing citrus. For the price, its ridiculous. Overall i'd rate this a 3/10, do not blind buy. PDM is a very hit or miss house.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62101"comment_id="2318793"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Greenley-62101.html?ccid=2318793#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2316695" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
I really cannot recommend Greenley at the niche price, there are so many cheaper and at least as good smelling if not better options.<br />
<br />

Maybe, just maybe a wealthy teen might like this?  This is not my 1st PDM.  Carlise, Layton, and Seedly are all great.<br />
Greely is NOT a safe blind buy.  Get a sample or go to a retailer to try.  Don't spray on your skin...use a card 1st or you'll walk around smelling like a nuclear Irish Spring soap bomb.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62101"comment_id="2224613"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Greenley-62101.html?ccid=2224613#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2222919" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It doesn’t wow me though. I get the comparison to apple shampoo, but it’s not that cheap or synthetic smelling. <br />
<br />
It sits somewhere in between Green Irish Tweed and the juicier Original Vetiver by Creed. It’s a fresh scent that is heavy on green apple, is juicy and effervescent, woody, and can be worn day or night. Longevity and projection were both moderate. If you like Apple and some wood, it’s a buy. But for me, I think I can live through summer without having regrets of not owning this.<br />
<br />
I chose to buy Percival over this, as percival just has one of the best fresh woods smells I’ve inhaled. <br />
I liken that to Green Irish Tweeds brother. Except it’s just in the blue realm.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62101"comment_id="2210457"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Greenley-62101.html?ccid=2210457#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2209084" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It is a PDM fragrance, they arent known for insanely unique compositions. It is a mass-appealing, well-formulated, fresh but complex green fragrance with a nice woody/musky dry down. In my opinion, the opening is a little bit synthetic, however after literally 15-20 min it becomes a very well-blended smell. padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2173249" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="ethan-fragrantica"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1673973"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="ethan-fragrantica" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2173249ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2173249" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.86); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1673973">ethan-fragrantica</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-31">05/31/24 04:14</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Greenley by Parfums de Marly: <br />
A really fresh green citrus that remains quite unique, it's the best of the PdM that I've tried so far and the apple in the opening give it a juicy vibe rather than earthy/herbal. The lemon and orange are present and balance the apple nicely. There is definitely a niche quality to this but performance is average. I get cedar and petitgrain before it dries down to more woody, mossy notes. It does smell like citrusy wet grass but in a good way.<br />
<br />
Top notes: Juicy apple, lemon, orange<br />
Middle notes: Cedar, petitgrain, violet<br />
Base notes: Oakmoss, woods<br />
<br />
Longevity: 3.5/5<br />
Sillage: 3/5<br />
Scent: 3.5/5<br />
Design: 4/5<br />
Gender: Unisex-Masculine<br />
Overall: 3.5/5</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62101"comment_id="2173249"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Greenley-62101.html?ccid=2173249#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2172803" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Oops, something happened in this bottle in the past couple of days. I didn't think it was that strong. <br />
I don't get compliments often, as for PDM, only once previously by a woman while I was wearing Herod. So to get 3 in 10 minutes from friends that know me as the dumbass that spends too much on cologne,  is kind of a big deal. Almost all of my compliments come from designer scents, but those are made to be mass appealing.<br />
<br />
 I guess this is a win for the house of PDM. It  now has 4 compliments out of 5 bottles lol. I don't care about compliments, I usually wear what I like, and only wear mass appealing stuff when I am going to large gatherings. I am going to dial the greenly back a bit, closer to my normal 6 sprays. But I have been experimenting with spraying heavy with the freshies and it has got some attention. I never wanted to be known as "that guy", you know... Nice crisp green apple opening which I love. One of my favorite openings from any fragrance I have tried and it is certainly unique while also being appealing. My only issue with the fragrance comes in the dry down, where as the apple begins to fade, I get a hint of a hand sanitizer/isopropyl alcohol smell which borderline ruins the wearing experience for me. Longevity is above average, I get around 6 hours, sillage is decent and projects off of me for about an hour, rarely two. If it wasn't overpriced and the dry down wasn't as harsh, it would be my go to summer fragrance. Potentially 2.5oz worthy, but I will be saving my money for an alternative. <br />
<br />
Scent: 8.2/10<br />
Longevity: 8.8/10<br />
Sillage: 8/10<br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2120921">zIGMA</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-04">05/04/24 12:54</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>TLDR; <br />
&gt;  Apple opener is fantastic, dry down is awfully synthetic.<br />
<br />
Longevity: Moderate<br />
Sillage: Moderate<br />
Gender: Unisex<br />
Price Value: Way overpriced<br />
<br />
Such a great green apple opener note and slightly ozonic. This was one of the few fragrances that I said, "I NEED this" when I smelled it at the store. Rarely do I smile when I smell a fragrance, but this was one of those times. So I'm heartbroken when I sprayed it on skin and tested to see how it develops. LOVE the opener, but the dry down is an abomination to me. It's SO synthetic, so much so that it makes it unwearable. Wanted to like this one so bad but it's just too synthetic that it overpowers any other notes in there for me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62101"comment_id="2145666"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Greenley-62101.html?ccid=2145666#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2144717" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Not anything like I expected. No discernable green apple, a bit sour on my skin. If I had been given this note breakdown, or ingredient list, my brain would have this in a very grassy, woodsy, leafy yet airy and bright style. It comes across much more synthetic in nature than I was expecting from a fragrance at this price point. None of them are reasonably priced for what they are, If I'm being honest. I've tested many PDM offerings, and when I look at what they retail for, It strikes me as absurdity. Performance on my skin was less than stellar, but that seems to be a trend and not something exclusive to me. I recommend sampling, of course, or at least hitting up your local PDM retailer and trying it yourself beforehand as I don't think the note breakdown really matches what is coming out of the sprayer. Just my opinion, of course, and YMMV.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62101"comment_id="2141664"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Greenley-62101.html?ccid=2141664#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2140146" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I smelled this at a Nordstrom and it was great on the test strip. Had this grassy, citrusy, woodsy element that reminded me of a bright green forest with the sunshine shining through the leaves. I went and bought a full bottle and the way it wore on my skin was much different. padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2123803" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Maya lilac"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1705079"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1705079.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Maya lilac" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2123803ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2123803" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.71); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1705079">Maya lilac</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-13">04/13/24 13:20</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>A higher end and more complex, slightly more masculine version of D&amp;G Light Blue Intense. <br />
Doesn’t smell bad at all, it’s quite mass appealing scent wise but not for Parfums de Marly price point.<br />
<br />
Me, as a woman, I would happily wear Greenley but if I could get it half off or something. It’s a fresh, citrusy, green scent, as the bottle or the name suggests with musk, cedar and cashmeran. No fuss, no frills, easy reach, grab and go for hot, humid days.  Cannot fault it, it is very natural smelling, super invigorating, crisp, green apple and petit grain, sweet mandarin and sparkling bergamot. Then it moves into a more woody, powdery, softer core before getting to a very clean, white musk and warm amber.<br />
<br />
 Has a bit of complexity and depth but in the end it’s not unique or strong enough to justify  255 euro per full size bottle in my opinion. If you have unlimited budget to splurge on everything, I wouldn’t say no, don’t buy it, it’s a bad fragrance. It’s not, it’s nice, very likeable but quite simple and it would get you compliments in the summertime high temperatures for sure!<br />
<br />
As for me, I will stick to my D&amp;G Intense for women and other green, fresher scents I already have because where I live, summer is basically nonexistent and I have already enough perfume for those very rare days!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2084469">dr3wski</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-11">04/11/24 09:29</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I was looking for a fantastic fresh summer fragrance and had seen many people doing reviews say they recommended Greenley. As I did more research it seemed like people were split about it, some saying it smelled cheap and wasn't worth the price, some saying it was fantastic. I agree with the latter. Very fresh, clean, versatile scent that I enjoy and am looking forward to wearing. I love the green apple note. I don't think that Greenley smells generic as some people say; an apple shampoo or hand soap, I think it is slightly synthetic but I wouldn't call it a cleanser type of smell. The performance is great for a fresh fragrance- about 8 hours of noticeable longevity and arms-length sillage for the first 2 hours or so.<br />
<br />
Edit: I'll be honest, Greenley isn't doing it for me anymore. I love the opening as I can smell the green apple blasting through but the dry down (as it starts to fade) just isn't it. I am picking up this dominating alcohol smell, like a cheap hand sanitizer. Not even Germ-X smell, I mean just straight Isopropyl alcohol. Very offputting. Although Greenley has better performance I think I will be choosing Sedley for this summer. <br />
<br />
Scent- 8.8/10<br />
Longevity- 9/10<br />
Sillage- 8/10<br />
Price- 6/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62101"comment_id="2121438"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Greenley-62101.html?ccid=2121438#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2121325" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2109374" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="3ak"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1740934"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1740934.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="3ak" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2109374ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2109374" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.79); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1740934">3ak</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-30">03/30/24 20:37</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is good but overpriced. Parfums de Marley is marketed brand. They have upper tier designer quality at niche pricing. They hit it big because of influencers and social media hype. Greenley is nice, alittle synthetic but nice. I do enjoy fruity fragrances. This is woody and fruity with a shampoo like vibe. The green apple shampoo vibe is pleasant. It's kind of like luxury soap feeling. The performance is good, about 8-9 hours. If PDM was priced like Mancera there wouldn't be an issue. Problem is this retails for like $350. I picked up a 75ml for about $120-$130 on discounters last year. At that price it's fine because that's basically what most designers retail at. I could only recommend this if you find it on discounters for under $150. If you're looking for a fresh green fruity fragrance this is very nice and will fulfill that role. I wore this quite a bit last spring and summer. Just don't over pay and wait until a sale on a discounter.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62101"comment_id="2109374"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Greenley-62101.html?ccid=2109374#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2104779" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />

I prefer to just smell this out the bottle as soon as you wear it then it's not the same fragrance you're basically just wearing a spicy wood fragrance the moment you spray it on yourself because that apple is gone <br />
<br />
Still up there with the best apple fragrances like PDM greenley, Kajal Dahab, Sora Dora Jahny, Kenneth Cole Reaction, DKNY be delicious, Spicebomb night vision, Bond no 9 lafayette street, Kayali eden apple, Jaguar classic black, Boss bottled no 6.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1680569">Skyway</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-13">02/13/24 19:40</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Like a lot of reviews before mine, this did somewhat of a 180 and grew on me so much. I got a sample and when first spraying it on, the opening was rather harsh and off-putting. I got a lot of the apple and didn't really care for it. As it dried down it got more pleasant but I had already written it off. I gave it another go about a week later and found myself enjoying it more. The opening is still a lot to me but after about 20 minutes it settles into a very refreshing, casual scent. This was during the February "winter" in Florida. A few days later the temp was in the 80s so I gave it a wear before biking in the park. I felt like I hit the jackpot on a scent for weather that dominates 80% of the year down here.<br />
<br />
Definitely a warm weather fragrance for spring and summer. Could definitely wear it in the fall, but in Florida that is really just extended summer. I'd go for something else once the weather starts getting colder. Daytime casual is the name of the game here. I feel like it is too playful for formal, office, or night wear but its not impossible to pull off in those situations. Performance is good for my skin. 2 sprays each to the chest and inner elbow got me 5-7 hours, although I need to test it more once the warm weather is here to stay. Will try to update once my bottle comes in!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62101"comment_id="2061521"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Greenley-62101.html?ccid=2061521#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2060067" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Clean woods and soft musks. That's really what you get. Classy, clean and masculine. <br />
Perfect for everyday use to school, work or gym as it's not too heavy or monstrous in projection, you'll have a nice little scent bubble with this on you. It's one of my go-to school and gym scents.<br />
Nothing groundbreaking here, but just with other PDM's, they have perfected the art of making extremely likeable, VERY high quality and easy going scents, without them being synthetic, harsh or familiar (Something very challenging in perfumery.) <br />
<br />
You will smell like a fresh and clean evergreen forest on a bright and airy day with this on. Its beautiful stuff.<br />
Highly recommend, one of my most worn scents in my collection for sure. This will work great even down to 50 degree days.<br />
I would recommend waiting for a tester of this to pop on a discounter, you could get 125ml for like $150. <br />
9/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62101"comment_id="2053190"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Greenley-62101.html?ccid=2053190#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2050847" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;     <div class="grid-x grid-padding-x grid-margin-y" style="position: relative; padding: 0 0.25rem 0 0.25rem;">
                            <div id="parent1624825" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1624825" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Rotten Rebel"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1327902"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1327902.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Rotten Rebel" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1624825ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck6x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1624825" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.79); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1327902">Rotten Rebel</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-08-16">08/16/22 09:21</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I just did a review of Greenley on my Youtube "Rotten Rebel" and like always I wanted to share my thoughts on it with the fine folks of Fragrantica!<br />
<br />
Greenley (to my nose) opens up with a crisp and fresh dose of apple and citrus together with a smooth woody side and as it dries down the woody side of it gets more prominent and more full and the citrus gets softer and the blend turns a bit green, musky and slightly powdery.<br />
<br />
At the core of it, from the opening to the end is that fantastic scent of sweet green apple together with smooth woodiness and I truly enjoy it.<br />
<br />
Greenley is so easy to wear and so easy to like. Well-made fragrances that focus on the scent of Apple are hard to find and this is at the top.. This to me is a freshie with a twist (that apple) and I like it a lot.<br />
<br />
My one (and only) issue with it is the performance.. It stays on my skin for A LONG time, but the projection is not the best... So after an hour or so I always feel the need to spray more.. And then more and more.. <br />
<br />
Overall a great fresh scent!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62101"comment_id="1624825"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Greenley-62101.html?ccid=1624825#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1202586" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I'll be getting a backup bottle of this fantastic juice.<br />

Scent: 9/10<br />
Longevity:10/10<br />
Projection: 8/10<br />
Price/Performance Ratio: 4/10 (until it reaches discounters)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62101"comment_id="1202586"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Greenley-62101.html?ccid=1202586#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1717354" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; as previously mentioned in negative comments "this smells like a cheap apple shampoo" that is not wrong at all. it does. but i genuinely do not find that to be a bad thing, its a great smell. simple and linear? yes. worth the money? thats completely up to you. <br />
if you are someone that buys niche for the fact that its something different and fancy, this one is not for you. it doesnt smell expensive, its not complex. its a very simple yet beautiful, delicious, apple smell.<br />
if you are looking for something fresh, bright, clean, and easy to wear for the warmer months, this is great!<br />
if you are looking for something different and that doesn't smell synthetic at all, this is not for you.<br />
i love it though and it does remind me of an apple shampoo i used as a kid. maybe the main reason i enjoy it is its nostalgic for me.<br />
if you are a fragrance snob and only want the best of the best, or try and pull off the most crazy, complex scents, this should probably be a pass for you.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62101"comment_id="1517357"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Greenley-62101.html?ccid=1517357#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="62101" sentiment="positive"></reviews-infinity>

Also, there is nothing that smells especially natural here. That alone doesn't have to be a negative quality but I just wonder about people here in the comments saying it smells natural. That's crazy to me. Doubt I'll finish the rest of my 10ml decant, life is too short to wear something you don't love.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62101"comment_id="1656890"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Greenley-62101.html?ccid=1656890#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2008490" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2008490" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Kyer"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1842538"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1842538.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Kyer" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/The-Harmonist/Hypnotizing-Fire-36700.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.36700.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Hypnotizing Fire"title="Hypnotizing Fire"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2008490ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2008490" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.8); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1842538">Kyer</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-12-23">12/23/23 00:06</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Edit: It grows on you, now I do smell the apple and I love it, it’s a fantastic fragrance and will definitely be on my top for summer. Never mind everything I said below lol. <br />
<br />
While I liked it, in my nose it kind of reminds me of Creed Aventus and what I mean by this is that the bergamot found in this really resembles Aventus and it’s 100 thousand clones. <br />
<br />
The bad thing is that I can only smell the bergamot and green notes, which is something not bad by itself, in fact they work good but since I’m not the biggest fan of bergamot it is kind of a let down, specially cause I think that every time bergamot it’s in the top 4 notes of a fragrance that’s pretty much all I can smell, bergamot is extremely strong in any fragrance, which again, is not bad by itself but kind of makes all fresh fragrances smell the same. <br />
<br />
I expected much more from the apple as well, I can’t smell any apple at all in this fragrance, like I said, it smells like a really fresh and green bergamot, but in my opinion or at least experience, the apple is not there at all.<br />
<br />
Final impression:<br />
<br />
Great summer green fragrance, longevity and projection are good. However, apple is not present at all, and personally because I’m not a fan of bergamot if I tested before buying I would’ve probably checked out something else. But leaving my bias towards bergamot to the side, it is a good fragrance, maybe just not worth the price.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62101"comment_id="2008490"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Greenley-62101.html?ccid=2008490#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="62101" sentiment="negative"></reviews-infinity>
